{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01VGcahT5fTVLmko38hf74mW","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01Ud7cj57dedZodhHrM9khTD","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/regression_test.py","content":"\"\"\"Regression test for HSV color percentage parsing bug.\n\nThis test demonstrates the bug where HSV colors specified with percentage values\nincorrectly scale the hue channel to 255 instead of 359.\n\nThe bug was that percentage values were always scaled using 255, but hue in HSV\ncolor space should be 0-359 degrees. So:\n- hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) should be (359, 255, 255) not (255, 255, 255)\n- hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) should be (~179, 127, 127) not (127, 127, 127)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtGui import QColor\n\n\nclass HsvColorParser:\n    \"\"\"Buggy HSV color parser that scales hue to 255 instead of 359.\"\"\"\n\n    def _parse_value_buggy(self, val: str) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Parse color value with the bug - always scales to 255.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return int(val)\n        except ValueError:\n            pass\n\n        # BUG: Always uses 255.0 as multiplier, even for hue\n        mult = 255.0\n        if val.endswith('%'):\n            val = val[:-1]\n            mult = 255.0 / 100\n            return int(float(val) * 255.0 / 100.0)\n\n        try:\n            return int(float(val) * mult)\n        except ValueError:\n            raise ValueError(f\"must be a valid color value: {val}\")\n\n    def _parse_value_fixed(self, kind: str, val: str) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Parse color value with the fix - scales hue to 359.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return int(val)\n        except ValueError:\n            pass\n\n        # FIXED: Use 359 for hue, 255 for other channels\n        mult = 359.0 if kind == 'h' else 255.0\n        if val.endswith('%'):\n            val = val[:-1]\n            mult = mult / 100\n\n        try:\n            return int(float(val) * mult)\n        except ValueError:\n            raise ValueError(f\"must be a valid color value: {val}\")\n\n    def parse_hsv_buggy(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSV color with the buggy implementation.\"\"\"\n        # All values go through the buggy parser\n        h = self._parse_value_buggy(h_str)\n        s = self._parse_value_buggy(s_str)\n        v = self._parse_value_buggy(v_str)\n        return (h, s, v)\n\n    def parse_hsv_fixed(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSV color with the fixed implementation.\"\"\"\n        # Each value uses the correct multiplier for its kind\n        h = self._parse_value_fixed('h', h_str)\n        s = self._parse_value_fixed('s', s_str)\n        v = self._parse_value_fixed('v', v_str)\n        return (h, s, v)\n\n    def parse_hsva_buggy(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str, a_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSVA color with the buggy implementation.\"\"\"\n        h, s, v = self.parse_hsv_buggy(h_str, s_str, v_str)\n        a = self._parse_value_buggy(a_str)\n        return (h, s, v, a)\n\n    def parse_hsva_fixed(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str, a_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSVA color with the fixed implementation.\"\"\"\n        h, s, v = self.parse_hsv_fixed(h_str, s_str, v_str)\n        a = self._parse_value_fixed('a', a_str)\n        return (h, s, v, a)\n\n\nclass TestHsvColorPercentageParsing:\n    \"\"\"Test HSV color percentage parsing for the bug.\"\"\"\n\n    def setup_method(self):\n        \"\"\"Set up the parser for each test.\"\"\"\n        self.parser = HsvColorParser()\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_buggy_vs_fixed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that 100% hue is incorrectly parsed as 255 (buggy) vs 359 (fixed).\"\"\"\n        # With the bug, 100% hue should parse to 255\n        h_buggy, s_buggy, v_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsv_buggy('100%', '100%', '100%')\n        assert h_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% hue to 255\"\n        assert s_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% saturation to 255\"\n        assert v_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% value to 255\"\n\n        # With the fix, 100% hue should parse to 359\n        h_fixed, s_fixed, v_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsv_fixed('100%', '100%', '100%')\n        assert h_fixed == 359, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% hue to 359\"\n        assert s_fixed == 255, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% saturation to 255\"\n        assert v_fixed == 255, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% value to 255\"\n\n        # The bug produces different colors for hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) vs hsv(359, 255, 255)\n        assert h_buggy != h_fixed, \"Hue values should differ between buggy and fixed\"\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_buggy_vs_fixed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that 50% hue is incorrectly parsed as 127 (buggy) vs 179 (fixed).\"\"\"\n        # With the bug, 50% hue should parse to 127-128\n        h_buggy, s_buggy, v_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsv_buggy('50%', '50%', '50%')\n        assert h_buggy == 127, \"Buggy parser should scale 50% hue to 127\"\n        assert s_buggy == 127, \"Buggy parser should scale 50% saturation to 127\"\n        assert v_buggy == 127, \"Buggy parser should scale 50% value to 127\"\n\n        # With the fix, 50% hue should parse to 179-180\n        h_fixed, s_fixed, v_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsv_fixed('50%', '50%', '50%')\n        assert h_fixed == 179, \"Fixed parser should scale 50% hue to 179\"\n        assert s_fixed == 127, \"Fixed parser should scale 50% saturation to 127\"\n        assert v_fixed == 127, \"Fixed parser should scale 50% value to 127\"\n\n        # The bug produces different colors\n        assert h_buggy != h_fixed, \"Hue values should differ between buggy and fixed\"\n        # But saturation and value should be the same (both always scaled to 255)\n        assert s_buggy == s_fixed, \"Saturation should be the same\"\n        assert v_buggy == v_fixed, \"Value should be the same\"\n\n    def test_hsva_100_percent_hue_buggy_vs_fixed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that HSVA with 100% hue is incorrectly parsed (buggy vs fixed).\"\"\"\n        # With the bug, 100% hue in HSVA should parse to 255\n        h_buggy, s_buggy, v_buggy, a_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsva_buggy(\n            '100%', '100%', '100%', '100%'\n        )\n        assert h_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% hue in HSVA to 255\"\n        assert a_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% alpha to 255\"\n\n        # With the fix, 100% hue in HSVA should parse to 359\n        h_fixed, s_fixed, v_fixed, a_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsva_fixed(\n            '100%', '100%', '100%', '100%'\n        )\n        assert h_fixed == 359, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% hue in HSVA to 359\"\n        assert a_fixed == 255, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% alpha to 255\"\n\n        # 100% should map to:\n        # - Buggy: 255 (scaling with 255.0 / 100)\n        # - Fixed: 359 (scaling with 359.0 / 100)\n\n        buggy_100 = int(100 * 255.0 / 100.0)  # = 255\n        fixed_100 = int(100 * 359.0 / 100.0)  # = 359\n\n        assert buggy_100 == 255, \"Buggy formula: 100% * 255.0 / 100.0 = 255\"\n        assert fixed_100 == 359, \"Fixed formula: 100% * 359.0 / 100.0 = 359\"\n        assert buggy_100 != fixed_100, \"The bug produces different scaling\"\n\n    def test_hue_degrees_vs_255_scale(self):\n        \"\"\"Test various hue percentages to show the scaling difference.\"\"\"\n        test_cases = [\n            ('0%', 0, 0),       # 0% -> (0, 0)\n            ('25%', 63, 89),    # 25% -> (63.75~64 buggy, 89.75~89 fixed)\n            ('50%', 127, 179),  # 50% -> (127.5~127 buggy, 179.5~179 fixed)\n            ('75%', 191, 269),  # {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Xcva7bB3iChdonJXsEbx1C","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_019jxHN253rzFC3rhYPyWWFN","name":"Bash","input":{"command":"python3 << 'PYTHON_EOF'\nimport os\n\ntest_content = '''\"\"\"Regression test for HSV color percentage parsing bug.\n\nThis test demonstrates the bug where HSV colors specified with percentage values\nincorrectly scale the hue channel to 255 instead of 359.\n\nThe bug was that percentage values were always scaled using 255, but hue in HSV\ncolor space should be 0-359 degrees. So:\n- hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) should be (359, 255, 255) not (255, 255, 255)\n- hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) should be (~179, 127, 127) not (127, 127, 127)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtGui import QColor\n\n\nclass HsvColorParser:\n    \"\"\"Buggy HSV color parser that scales hue to 255 instead of 359.\"\"\"\n\n    def _parse_value_buggy(self, val: str) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Parse color value with the bug - always scales to 255.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return int(val)\n        except ValueError:\n            pass\n\n        # BUG: Always uses 255.0 as multiplier, even for hue\n        mult = 255.0\n        if val.endswith('%'):\n            val = val[:-1]\n            mult = 255.0 / 100\n            return int(float(val) * 255.0 / 100.0)\n\n        try:\n            return int(float(val) * mult)\n        except ValueError:\n            raise ValueError(f\"must be a valid color value: {val}\")\n\n    def _parse_value_fixed(self, kind: str, val: str) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Parse color value with the fix - scales hue to 359.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return int(val)\n        except ValueError:\n            pass\n\n        # FIXED: Use 359 for hue, 255 for other channels\n        mult = 359.0 if kind == 'h' else 255.0\n        if val.endswith('%'):\n            val = val[:-1]\n            mult = mult / 100\n\n        try:\n            return int(float(val) * mult)\n        except ValueError:\n            raise ValueError(f\"must be a valid color value: {val}\")\n\n    def parse_hsv_buggy(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSV color with the buggy implementation.\"\"\"\n        # All values go through the buggy parser\n        h = self._parse_value_buggy(h_str)\n        s = self._parse_value_buggy(s_str)\n        v = self._parse_value_buggy(v_str)\n        return (h, s, v)\n\n    def parse_hsv_fixed(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSV color with the fixed implementation.\"\"\"\n        # Each value uses the correct multiplier for its kind\n        h = self._parse_value_fixed('h', h_str)\n        s = self._parse_value_fixed('s', s_str)\n        v = self._parse_value_fixed('v', v_str)\n        return (h, s, v)\n\n    def parse_hsva_buggy(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str, a_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSVA color with the buggy implementation.\"\"\"\n        h, s, v = self.parse_hsv_buggy(h_str, s_str, v_str)\n        a = self._parse_value_buggy(a_str)\n        return (h, s, v, a)\n\n    def parse_hsva_fixed(self, h_str: str, s_str: str, v_str: str, a_str: str):\n        \"\"\"Parse HSVA color with the fixed implementation.\"\"\"\n        h, s, v = self.parse_hsv_fixed(h_str, s_str, v_str)\n        a = self._parse_value_fixed('a', a_str)\n        return (h, s, v, a)\n\n\nclass TestHsvColorPercentageParsing:\n    \"\"\"Test HSV color percentage parsing for the bug.\"\"\"\n\n    def setup_method(self):\n        \"\"\"Set up the parser for each test.\"\"\"\n        self.parser = HsvColorParser()\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_buggy_vs_fixed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that 100% hue is incorrectly parsed as 255 (buggy) vs 359 (fixed).\"\"\"\n        # With the bug, 100% hue should parse to 255\n        h_buggy, s_buggy, v_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsv_buggy('100%', '100%', '100%')\n        assert h_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% hue to 255\"\n        assert s_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% saturation to 255\"\n        assert v_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% value to 255\"\n\n        # With the fix, 100% hue should parse to 359\n        h_fixed, s_fixed, v_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsv_fixed('100%', '100%', '100%')\n        assert h_fixed == 359, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% hue to 359\"\n        assert s_fixed == 255, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% saturation to 255\"\n        assert v_fixed == 255, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% value to 255\"\n\n        # The bug produces different colors for hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) vs hsv(359, 255, 255)\n        assert h_buggy != h_fixed, \"Hue values should differ between buggy and fixed\"\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_buggy_vs_fixed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that 50% hue is incorrectly parsed as 127 (buggy) vs 179 (fixed).\"\"\"\n        # With the bug, 50% hue should parse to 127-128\n        h_buggy, s_buggy, v_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsv_buggy('50%', '50%', '50%')\n        assert h_buggy == 127, \"Buggy parser should scale 50% hue to 127\"\n        assert s_buggy == 127, \"Buggy parser should scale 50% saturation to 127\"\n        assert v_buggy == 127, \"Buggy parser should scale 50% value to 127\"\n\n        # With the fix, 50% hue should parse to 179-180\n        h_fixed, s_fixed, v_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsv_fixed('50%', '50%', '50%')\n        assert h_fixed == 179, \"Fixed parser should scale 50% hue to 179\"\n        assert s_fixed == 127, \"Fixed parser should scale 50% saturation to 127\"\n        assert v_fixed == 127, \"Fixed parser should scale 50% value to 127\"\n\n        # The bug produces different colors\n        assert h_buggy != h_fixed, \"Hue values should differ between buggy and fixed\"\n        # But saturation and value should be the same (both always scaled to 255)\n        assert s_buggy == s_fixed, \"Saturation should be the same\"\n        assert v_buggy == v_fixed, \"Value should be the same\"\n\n    def test_hsva_100_percent_hue_buggy_vs_fixed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that HSVA with 100% hue is incorrectly parsed (buggy vs fixed).\"\"\"\n        # With the bug, 100% hue in HSVA should parse to 255\n        h_buggy, s_buggy, v_buggy, a_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsva_buggy(\n            '100%', '100%', '100%', '100%'\n        )\n        assert h_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% hue in HSVA to 255\"\n        assert a_buggy == 255, \"Buggy parser should scale 100% alpha to 255\"\n\n        # With the fix, 100% hue in HSVA should parse to 359\n        h_fixed, s_fixed, v_fixed, a_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsva_fixed(\n            '100%', '100%', '100%', '100%'\n        )\n        assert h_fixed == 359, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% hue in HSVA to 359\"\n        assert a_fixed == 255, \"Fixed parser should scale 100% alpha to 255\"\n\n        # The bug produces different hue values\n        assert h_buggy != h_fixed, \"Hue values should differ between buggy and fixed\"\n\n    def test_hsva_50_percent_hue_buggy_vs_fixed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that HSVA with 50% hue is incorrectly parsed (buggy vs fixed).\"\"\"\n        # With the bug\n        h_buggy, s_buggy, v_buggy, a_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsva_buggy(\n            '50%', '50%', '50%', '50%'\n        )\n        assert h_buggy == 127, \"Buggy parser should scale 50% hue in HSVA to 127\"\n\n        # With the fix\n        h_fixed, s_fixed, v_fixed, a_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsva_fixed(\n            '50%', '50%', '50%', '50%'\n        )\n        assert h_fixed == 179, \"Fixed parser should scale 50% hue in HSVA to 179\"\n\n        # The bug produces different hue values\n        assert h_buggy != h_fixed, \"Hue values should differ between buggy and fixed\"\n\n    def test_hue_scaling_difference(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that demonstrates the core scaling difference for hue.\"\"\"\n        # 100% should map to:\n        # - Buggy: 255 (scaling with 255.0 / 100)\n        # - Fixed: 359 (scaling with 359.0 / 100)\n\n        buggy_100 = int(100 * 255.0 / 100.0)  # = 255\n        fixed_100 = int(100 * 359.0 / 100.0)  # = 359\n\n        assert buggy_100 == 255, \"Buggy formula: 100% * 255.0 / 100.0 = 255\"\n        assert fixed_100 == 359, \"Fixed formula: 100% * 359.0 / 100.0 = 359\"\n        assert buggy_100 != fixed_100, \"The bug produces different scaling\"\n\n    def test_hue_degrees_vs_255_scale(self):\n        \"\"\"Test various hue percentages to show the scaling difference.\"\"\"\n        test_cases = [\n            ('0%', 0, 0),       # 0% -> (0, 0)\n            ('25%', 63, 89),    # 25% -> (63.75~64 buggy, 89.75~89 fixed)\n            ('50%', 127, 179),  # 50% -> (127.5~127 buggy, 179.5~179 fixed)\n            ('75%', 191, 269),  # 75% -> (191.25~191 buggy, 269.25~269 fixed)\n            ('100%', 255, 359), # 100% -> (255 buggy, 359 fixed)\n        ]\n\n        for percentage, expected_buggy, expected_fixed in test_cases:\n            h_buggy, _, _ = self.parser.parse_hsv_buggy(percentage, '0%', '0%')\n            h_fixed, _, _ = self.parser.parse_hsv_fixed(percentage, '0%', '0%')\n\n            assert h_buggy == expected_buggy, (\n                f\"{percentage} hue should parse to {expected_buggy} with bug\"\n            )\n            assert h_fixed == expected_fixed, (\n                f\"{percentage} hue should parse to {expected_fixed} with fix\"\n            )\n\n    def test_saturation_value_parsing_unaffected(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that saturation and value parsing are the same in both versions.\n\n        Both buggy and fixed versions use 255 for saturation and value,\n        so they should produce identical results for these channels.\n        \"\"\"\n        test_cases = ['0%', '25%', '50%', '75%', '100%']\n\n        for percentage in test_cases:\n            _, s_buggy, v_buggy = self.parser.parse_hsv_buggy(\n                '0%', percentage, percentage\n            )\n            _, s_fixed, v_fixed = self.parser.parse_hsv_fixed(\n                '0%', percentage, percentage\n            )\n\n            assert s_buggy == s_fixed, (\n                f\"Saturation should be the same for {percentage}: \"\n                f\"buggy={s_buggy}, fixed={s_fixed}\"\n            )\n            assert v_buggy == v_fixed, (\n                f\"Value should be the same for {percentage}: \"\n                f\"buggy={v_buggy}, fixed={v_fixed}\"\n            )\n\n    def test_absolute_values_unaffected(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that absolute (non-percentage) values work the same way.\"\"\"\n        #
